////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//		Tadb_RegV.txt : Complement to Tadb.txt containing
//					 	regulating valve definitions
//
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

new:CTable(RVTYPE_TAB\1) -> LIST_TAB
{
	"Regulating valve types"
	1						// 0/1: 1 if this table is the true parent of the IDs in it.
}

new:CTable(REGVALV_TAB\1) -> ROOT_TABLE
{
	"Regulating Valves"
	1						// 0/1: 1 if this table is the true parent of the IDs in it.
}

new:CTable(REGVACCGROUP_TAB) -> ROOT_TABLE
{
	"Regulating valve accessory groups"
	1						// 0/1: 1 if this table is the true parent of the IDs in it.
}

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//		Table VALVE_CHAR_TAB : Table of regulating valve characteristics
//
//	new:CDB_ValveCharacteristic(ID\1) -> VALVE_CHAR_TAB
//	{
//		{
//			Discrete/Continuous: 				#eDISCRETE_True, #eDISCRETE_False or #eDISCRETE_Undefined
//			Single/Multi/Electronic-turn: 		#eTURN_Single, #eTURN_Multi, #eTURN_Electronic or #eTURN_Undefined
//			SettingRounding						Allows to know how to round the result of a computing setting.
//		}
//		Min measurable setting (for TA-Scope)
//		Min recommended setting (for selection)
//		Number of curves
//		Opening 1 \ Kv catalogue [ \ Lambda \Re* \ Kv from test ]
//		Opening 2 \ Kv catalogue [ \ Lambda \Re* \ Kv from test ]
//		...
//	}
//


////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
// STAD
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//		Table REGVALV_TAB : Regulating valves
//
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//	How to write a regulating valve information ?
//	---------------------------------------------
//
//	new:CDB_RegulatingValve(ID)->REGVALV_TAB
//	{
//		{
//			{
//				{
//					{
//						0				isDeleted
//						1				isAvailable
//						0				isHidden
//						1				isFix
//						0				Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation)
//						0				Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc).
//      				0               Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
//					}
//					Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
//					PNRangeID			Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
//					Tmax in �C
//					Tmin in �C
//				}
//				"Reference"				Reference to the TA Product
//				"Name"					Name of the product
//				TypeID					Identifier of the valve type
//				FamilyID				Identifier of the family of the product
//				VersionID				Identifier of the version of the product
//				PriorityLevel			Level of priority for selection [1,10]
//				Comment					Product comment
//				ProdImgID				Product image ID
//				AccessGroupID			Identifier of the accessory group
//				PartOfaSet				Boolean indicating if the valve is part of a ActSet
//				TableSetID				Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
//				Price					Price of the product
// 				ProductUseFlag			#eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
//				AccessorySeriesID		Identifier of the series of the accessory
//				isAttached				0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately		
//   			AccTypeID				Identifier of Accessory type if #eBoth 
//				AccFamilyID				Identifier of Accessory family if #eBoth
//			}
//			BodyMaterialID			Identifier of the body material
//			SizeID					Identifier of the corresp. valve size
//			ConnectID				Identifier of the (inlet/pipe side) connection
//			ConnTabID				Identifier of the connection table, can be NO_ID
//			Conn2ID					Identifier of the outlet/body side connection, can be NO_ID
//			CBIType					Type of the valve as used in the CBI II
//			CBISize					Size of the valve as used in the CBI II
//			CBISizeInch				Size of the valve in inch as used in the CBI II
//			CBICompatibilityIndex	CBI compatibility Index
//			CBIVersion				CBI Version
//			Dpmax					Maximum Dp of the valve
//			MeasPt					Measuring points
//			MeasurableData			Measurable data
//			InletSizeID				Identifier of the inlet size ID
//			OutletSizeID			Identifier of the outlet size ID
//		}
//		CharactID		Identifier of the valve characteristic
//	}
// Inherited Fields
//	CDB_Thing::Deleted
//	CDB_Thing::Available
//	CDB_Thing::Hidden
//	CDB_Thing::Fixed
//	CDB_Thing::FreeInt1
//	CDB_Thing::FreeInt2
//	CDB_Thing::SortInt
//	CDB_HydroThing::Pmax
//	CDB_HydroThing::PNRange
//	CDB_HydroThing::Tmax
//	CDB_HydroThing::Tmin
//	CDB_Product::Reference
//	CDB_Product::Name
//  CDB_Product::TypeID
//	CDB_Product::FamilyID
//	CDB_Product::VersionID
//	CDB_Product::PriorityLevel
//	CDB_Product::Comment
//	CDB_Product::ProdImgID
//	CDB_Product::AccessGroupID
//	CDB_Product::PartOfaSet
//  CDB_Product::TableSetID
//	CDB_Product::Price
//	CDB_Product::ProductUseFlag
//	CDB_Product::AccessorySeriesID
//	CDB_Product::isAttached
//	CDB_Product::AccTypeID
//	CDB_Product::AccFamilyID
//	CDB_TAProduct::BodyMaterialID
//	CDB_TAProduct::SizeID
//	CDB_TAProduct::ConnectID
//	CDB_TAProduct::ConnTabID
//	CDB_TAProduct::Conn2ID
//	CDB_TAProduct::CBIType
//	CDB_TAProduct::CBISize
//	CDB_TAProduct::CBISizeInch
//  CDB_TAProduct::CBICompatibilityIndex
//	CDB_TAProduct::CBIVersion
//	CDB_TAProduct::Dpmax
//	CDB_TAProduct::MeasPt
//	CDB_TAProduct::MeasurableData
//	CDB_TAProduct::InletSizeID
//	CDB_TAProduct::OutletSizeID
//	CDB_RegulatingValve::CharactID
//
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////


//****************************
// Balancing Valves
//****************************

////////////////
// *** STAS ****
////////////////

new:CDB_RegulatingValve(STAS15_BV\1) -> REGVALV_TAB
{
	{
		{
			{
				{
					0															// isDeleted
					1                                                           // isAvailable
					0                                                           // isHidden
					1                                                           // isFix
					1                                                           // Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation)
					0                                                           // Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc).
					0               											// Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
				}
				0.6e+6 \ 2.0e+6                                 			// Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
				NO_ID                                                       // PNRangeID			Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
				120.0                                                       // Tmax in �C
				-20.0                                                       // Tmin in �C
			}
			"52151-914"                                         		// Reference to the TA Product
			"STAS 1/2""                                                 // Name of the product
			RVTYPE_BV                                                   // Identifier of the valve type
			FAM_STAS                                                    // Identifier of the family of the product
			VERS_NODRAIN                                                // Identifier of the version of the product
			1                                                           // Level of priority for selection [1,10]
			""                                                          // Product comment
			"TA_BV"                                                     // Product image ID
			ACCREGVGR_STAD_NODRAIN                                      // Identifier of the accessory group
			#ePartOfaSetNo                                              // Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
			NO_ID														// Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
			0.0                                                         // Price of the product
			#eProduct                              	                	// #eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
			NO_ID                                                   	// Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)
			0                                                       	// 0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately (for DlgDirSel)

// HYS-1847: STAG DN200-300 change family from FAM_STAG to FAM_STAG*_G
new:CDB_RegulatingValve(STAG200_BV\1) -> REGVALV_TAB
{
	{
		{
			{
				{
					0															// isDeleted
					1                                                           // isAvailable
					0                                                           // isHidden
					1                                                           // isFix
					1                                                           // Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation)
					0                                                           // Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc).
					0               											// Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
				}
				0.6e+6 \ 2.5e+6                                 			// Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
				NO_ID                                                       // PNRangeID			Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
				120.0                                                       // Tmax in �C
				-10.0                                                       // Tmin in �C
			}
			"52183-219"                                         		// Reference to the TA Product
			"STAG 200"                                                  // Name of the product
			RVTYPE_BV                                                   // Identifier of the valve type
			FAM_STAG*_G                                                 // Identifier of the family of the product
			VERS_STD                                                    // Identifier of the version of the product
			1                                                           // Level of priority for selection [1,10]
			""                                                          // Product comment
			"PX_STAG200_BV"                                             // Product image ID
			ACCSTAG200_400                                              // Identifier of the accessory group
			#ePartOfaSetNo                                              // Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
			NO_ID														// Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
			0.0                                                         // Price of the product
			#eProduct                              	                	// #eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
			NO_ID                                                   	// Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)
			0                                                       	// 0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately (for DlgDirSel)
			NO_ID                                      	            	// Identifier of the accessory type if #eBoth 
			NO_ID										            	// Identifier of the accessory family if #eBoth	
		}
		BDY_DUCTIRON                                            	// Identifier of the body material
		DN_200                                                       // Identifier of the corresp. valve size
		CONN_GROOVE                                                 // Identifier of the (inlet/pipe side) connection
		NO_ID                                                       // Identifier of the connection table, can be NO_ID
		NO_ID                                                       // Identifier of the outlet/body side connection, can be NO_ID
		"STAG"                                                      // Type of the valve as used in the CBI II
		"200"                                                       // Size of the valve as used in the CBI II
		"8"                                                         // Size of the valve in inch as used in the CBI II
		1                                                           // CBI compatibility Index
		"3A"                                                        // CBI Version
		0.0                                                         // Maximum Dp of the valve
		#eMeasPointInlet | #eMeasPointOutlet                        // Measuring points
		#eMeasDataDp | #eMeasDataFlow | #eMeasDataDpAvail           // Measurable data. #eMeasDataNone or a combination of #eMeasDataDp, #eMeasDataFlow, #eMeasDataDpSignal, #eMeasDataDpAvail, #eMeasDataDpStab or #eMeasDataDpCAlwaysOn.

		NO_ID                                                       // Identifier of the connection table, can be NO_ID
		NO_ID                                                       // Identifier of the outlet/body side connection, can be NO_ID

new:CDB_RegulatingValve(TA243-65A_BVS\1) -> REGVALV_TAB
{
	{
		{
			{
				{
					0															// isDeleted
					1                                                           // isAvailable
					0                                                           // isHidden
					1                                                           // isFix
					1                                                           // Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation)
					0                                                           // Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc).
					0               											// Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
				}
				1.6e+6 \ 1.6e+6                                 			// Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
				NO_ID                                                       // PNRangeID			Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
				200.0                                                       // Tmax in �C
				-20.0                                                       // Tmin in �C
			}
			"6-52243-065"                                       		// Reference to the TA Product
			"TA-BVS 243 DN65"                                           // Name of the product
			RVTYPE_BVSS                                                 // Identifier of the valve type
			FAM_TA243                                                   // Identifier of the family of the product
			VERS_FPM                                                    // Identifier of the version of the product
			1                                                           // Level of priority for selection [1,10]
			""                                                          // Product comment
			"TA_BV"                                                     // Product image ID
			NO_ID                                                       // Identifier of the accessory group
			#ePartOfaSetNo                                              // Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
			NO_ID														// Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
			0.0                                                         // Price of the product
			#eProduct                              	                	// #eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
			NO_ID                                                   	// Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)
			0                                                       	// 0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately (for DlgDirSel)
			NO_ID                                      	            	// Identifier of the accessory type if #eBoth 
			NO_ID										            	// Identifier of the accessory family if #eBoth	
		}
		BDY_STSTEEL                                             	// Identifier of the body material
		DN_65                                                       // Identifier of the corresp. valve size
		CONN_FLANGE                                                 // Identifier of the (inlet/pipe side) connection
		NO_ID                                                       // Identifier of the connection table, can be NO_ID
		NO_ID                                                       // Identifier of the outlet/body side connection, can be NO_ID
		"TA 243"                                                    // Type of the valve as used in the CBI II
		"65"                                                        // Size of the valve as used in the CBI II
		"2 1/2"                                                     // Size of the valve in inch as used in the CBI II
		1                                                           // CBI compatibility Index
		"3C"                                                        // CBI Version
		0.0                                                         // Maximum Dp of the valve
		#eMeasPointInlet | #eMeasPointOutlet                        // Measuring points
		#eMeasDataDp | #eMeasDataFlow | #eMeasDataDpAvail           // Measurable data. #eMeasDataNone or a combination of #eMeasDataDp, #eMeasDataFlow, #eMeasDataDpSignal, #eMeasDataDpAvail, #eMeasDataDpStab or #eMeasDataDpCAlwaysOn.
		NO_ID														// Identifier of the inlet size ID
		NO_ID														// Identifier of the outlet size ID
	}
	C_TA240-65                                                  // Identifier of the valve characteristic
}

					1                                                           // isFix
					1                                                           // Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation)
					0                                                           // Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc).
					0               											// Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
				}
				2.5e+6 \ 2.5e+6                                 			// Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
				NO_ID                                                       // PNRangeID			Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
				120.0                                                       // Tmax in �C
				-20.0                                                       // Tmin in �C
			}
			"6-52250-015"                                       		// Reference to the TA Product
			"TA-BVS* 240 DN15"                                          // Name of the product
			RVTYPE_BVSS                                                 // Identifier of the valve type
			FAM_TA240                                                   // Identifier of the family of the product
			VERS_FPM                                                    // Identifier of the version of the product
			1                                                           // Level of priority for selection [1,10]
			""                                                          // Product comment
			"TA_BV"                                                     // Product image ID
			NO_ID                                                       // Identifier of the accessory group
			#ePartOfaSetNo                                              // Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
			NO_ID														// Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
			0.0                                                         // Price of the product
			#eProduct                              	                	// #eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
			NO_ID                                                   	// Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)
			0                                                       	// 0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately (for DlgDirSel)
			NO_ID                                      	            	// Identifier of the accessory type if #eBoth 
			NO_ID										            	// Identifier of the accessory family if #eBoth	
		}
		BDY_STSTEEL                                             	// Identifier of the body material
		DN_15                                                       // Identifier of the corresp. valve size
		CONN_WELDING                                                // Identifier of the (inlet/pipe side) connection
		NO_ID                                                       // Identifier of the connection table, can be NO_ID
		NO_ID                                                       // Identifier of the outlet/body side connection, can be NO_ID
		"TA 240"                                                    // Type of the valve as used in the CBI II
		"15"                                                        // Size of the valve as used in the CBI II
		"1/2"                                                       // Size of the valve in inch as used in the CBI II
		1                                                           // CBI compatibility Index
		"3C"                                                        // CBI Version
		0.0                                                         // Maximum Dp of the valve
		#eMeasPointInlet | #eMeasPointOutlet                        // Measuring points
		#eMeasDataDp | #eMeasDataFlow | #eMeasDataDpAvail           // Measurable data. #eMeasDataNone or a combination of #eMeasDataDp, #eMeasDataFlow, #eMeasDataDpSignal, #eMeasDataDpAvail, #eMeasDataDpStab or #eMeasDataDpCAlwaysOn.
		NO_ID														// Identifier of the inlet size ID
		NO_ID														// Identifier of the outlet size ID
	}
	C_TA240*-15                                                  // Identifier of the valve characteristic

//
//		Table VALVE_CHAR_TAB : Table of regulating valve characteristics
//
//	new:CDB_ValveCharacteristic(ID\1) -> VALVE_CHAR_TAB
//	{
//		{
//			Discrete/Continuous: 				#eDISCRETE_True, #eDISCRETE_False or #eDISCRETE_Undefined
//			Single/Multi/Electronic-turn: 		#eTURN_Single, #eTURN_Multi, #eTURN_Electronic or #eTURN_Undefined
//			SettingRounding						Allows to know how to round the result of a computing setting.
//		}
//		Min measurable setting (for TA-Scope)
//		Min recommended setting (for selection)
//		Number of curves
//		opening 1 \ Kv 1
//		opening 2 \ Kv 2
//		...
//	}
//
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

	1.0                                     // Min recommended setting (for selection)

new:CDB_RegulatingValve(MULTI15A_BV\1) -> REGVALV_TAB
{
	{
		{
			{
				{
					0												// isDeleted
					1                                               // isAvailable
					0                                               // isHidden
					1                                               // isFix
					1                                               // Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation)
					0                                               // Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc).
					0               								// Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
				}
				1.6e+6 \ 1.6e+6                                 	// Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
				NO_ID                                               // PNRangeID			Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
				120.0                                               // Tmax in �C
				-10.0                                               // Tmin in �C
			}
			"5850-02.000"                                          	// Reference to the TA Product
			"TA-Multi 15"                                           // Name of the product
			RVTYPE_BV                                               // Identifier of the valve type
			FAM_MULTI_BV                                            // Identifier of the family of the product
			VERS_STD                                                // Identifier of the version of the product
			1                                                       // Level of priority for selection [1,10]
			""                                                      // Product comment
			"PX_TAMULTI20_BV"                                       // Product image ID
			ACCREGVGR_MULTIBV15_FT                                  // Identifier of the accessory group
			#ePartOfaSetNo                                          // Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
			NO_ID													// Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
			0.0                                                     // Price of the product
			#eProduct                              	                // #eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
			NO_ID                                                   // Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)
			0                                                       // 0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately (for DlgDirSel)
			NO_ID                                      	            // Identifier of the accessory type if #eBoth 
			NO_ID										            // Identifier of the accessory family if #eBoth	
		}
		BDY_GUNMETAL                                              	// Identifier of the body material
		DN_15                                                       // Identifier of the corresp. valve size
		CONN_THREAD                                                 // Identifier of the (inlet/pipe side) connection
		NO_ID                                                       // Identifier of the connection table, can be NO_ID
		NO_ID                                                       // Identifier of the outlet/body side connection, can be NO_ID
		""                                                     		// Type of the valve as used in the CBI II
		""                                                     		// Size of the valve as used in the CBI II
		""                                                    		// Size of the valve in inch as used in the CBI II
		1                                                           // CBI compatibility Index
		""                                                        	// CBI Version
		2.0e+5                                                      // Maximum Dp of the valve
		#eMeasPointInlet | #eMeasPointMeasStatOut                   // Measuring points
		#eMeasDataDpSignal | #eMeasDataFlow                         // Measurable data. #eMeasDataNone or a combination of #eMeasDataDp, #eMeasDataFlow, #eMeasDataDpSignal, #eMeasDataDpAvail, #eMeasDataDpStab or #eMeasDataDpCAlwaysOn.
		NO_ID														// Identifier of the inlet size ID
		NO_ID														// Identifier of the outlet size ID
	}
	C_MULTI_BV_15                                                 	// Identifier of the valve characteristic
}

new:CDB_FixedOrifice(TALOOP_2.36_FO\1) -> REGVALV_TAB
{
	{
		{
			{
				{
					0															// isDeleted
					1                                                           // isAvailable
					0                                                           // isHidden
					1                                                           // isFix
					1                                                           // Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation)
					0                                                           // Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc).
					0               											// Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
				}
				0.6e+6 \ 1.0e+6                                 			// Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
				NO_ID                                                       // PNRangeID			Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
				120.0                                                       // Tmax in �C
				-10.0                                                       // Tmin in �C
			}
			"50693-122"                                         		// Reference to the TA Product
			"TA Loop 2.36"                                              // Name of the product
			RVTYPE_FO                                                   // Identifier of the valve type
			FAM_TALOOP                                                  // Identifier of the family of the product
			VERS_STD                                                    // Identifier of the version of the product
			1                                                           // Level of priority for selection [1,10]
			""                                                          // Product comment
			"TA_FO"                                                     // Product image ID
			NO_ID                                                       // Identifier of the accessory group
			#ePartOfaSetNo                                              // Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
			NO_ID														// Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
			0.0                                                         // Price of the product
			#eProduct                              	                	// #eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
			NO_ID                                                   	// Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)
			0                                                       	// 0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately (for DlgDirSel)
			NO_ID                                      	            	// Identifier of the accessory type if #eBoth 
			NO_ID										            	// Identifier of the accessory family if #eBoth	
		}

new:CDB_VenturiValve(STAV15ULFA_VV\1) -> REGVALV_TAB
{
	{
		{
			{
				{
					0															// isDeleted
					1                                                           // isAvailable
					0                                                           // isHidden
					1                                                           // isFix
					1                                                           // Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation)
					0                                                           // Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc).
					0               											// Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
				}
				0.6e+6 \ 2.0e+6                                 			// Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
				NO_ID                                                       // PNRangeID			Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
				120.0                                                       // Tmax in �C
				-20.0                                                       // Tmin in �C
			}
			"52572-215"                                         		// Reference to the TA Product
			"STAV 15ULF"                                                // Name of the product
			RVTYPE_VV                                                   // Identifier of the valve type
			FAM_STAV                                                    // Identifier of the family of the product
			VERS_STD                                                    // Identifier of the version of the product
			1                                                           // Level of priority for selection [1,10]
			""                                                          // Product comment
			"TA_VV"                                                     // Product image ID
			NO_ID                                                       // Identifier of the accessory group
			#ePartOfaSetNo                                              // Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
			NO_ID														// Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
			0.0                                                         // Price of the product
			#eProduct                              	                	// #eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
			NO_ID                                                   	// Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)
			0                                                       	// 0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately (for DlgDirSel)
			NO_ID                                      	            	// Identifier of the accessory type if #eBoth 
			NO_ID										            	// Identifier of the accessory family if #eBoth	
		}
		BDY_AMETAL                                              	// Identifier of the body material
		DN_15                                                       // Identifier of the corresp. valve size
		CONN_THREAD                                                 // Identifier of the (inlet/pipe side) connection
		NO_ID                                                       // Identifier of the connection table, can be NO_ID
		NO_ID                                                       // Identifier of the outlet/body side connection, can be NO_ID
		"STAV"                                                      // Type of the valve as used in the CBI II
		"15ULF"                                                     // Size of the valve as used in the CBI II
		"1/2ULF"                                                    // Size of the valve in inch as used in the CBI II
		1                                                           // CBI compatibility Index
		"3D"                                                        // CBI Version
		0.0                                                         // Maximum Dp of the valve
		#eMeasPointInlet | #eMeasPointMeasStatOut                   // Measuring points
		#eMeasDataDpSignal | #eMeasDataFlow                         // Measurable data. #eMeasDataNone or a combination of #eMeasDataDp, #eMeasDataFlow, #eMeasDataDpSignal, #eMeasDataDpAvail, #eMeasDataDpStab or #eMeasDataDpCAlwaysOn.
		NO_ID														// Identifier of the inlet size ID
		NO_ID														// Identifier of the outlet size ID
	}
	C_VTRI15ULF                                                 // Identifier of the valve characteristic
	C_STAV15ULF
}

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//		Table ACCREGVGR_STAD : Regulating valve accessory groups
//
//		Rules:
//			ACXXXID \ &ACYYYID	// ACXXXID implies ACYYYID
//			ACXXXID \ !ACYYYID	// ACXXXID excludes ACYYYID
//			>ACXXXID			// ACXXXID is built-in
//			^ACXXXID			// ACXXXID excludes all others
//		  	*ACXXXID			// ACXXXID two pieces should be included
//			#ACXXXID			// ACXXXID is distributed on each parent item (3 vessels (1 primary + 2 secondary) => 3 times the accessory).
//			+ACXXXID 			// ACXXXID is an intersection between this group and an other. For this group accessory is NOT displayed
//			++ACXXXID			// ACXXXID is an intersection between this group and an other. For this group accessory is displayed
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

new:CDB_RuledTable(ACCREGVGR_STAD_NODRAIN) -> REGVACCGROUP_TAB
{
	{
		"STAD without drain"
		0						// 0/1: 1 if this table is the true parent of the IDs in it.
	}
	*ACRV1						// 52179-016: Extension for measuring point M14x1
	*ACRV2						// 52179-006: Self-sealing measuring point extension. Length 60 mm. Can be installed without draining of the system.
	ACRV3 \ !ACRV4				// 52179-990: Draining kit 1/2". Can be installed during system operation.
	ACRV4 \ !ACRV3				// 52179-996: Draining kit 3/4". Can be installed during system operation.
}

new:CDB_RuledTable(ACCRVGR_STAD_NODRAIN_US) -> REGVACCGROUP_TAB
{
	{
		"STAD without drain"
		0						// 0/1: 1 if this table is the true parent of the IDs in it.
	}
	*ACRV1						// 52179-016: Extension for measuring point M14x1. Length 71 mm. Suitable when insulation is used.
	*ACRV2						// 52179-006: Self-sealing measuring point extension. Length 60 mm. Can be installed without draining of the system.
	ACRV5						// 52179-997: Draining kit 3/4" NPS. Can be installed during system operation.
}
